{\huge\bfseries anubaMdha 1}

{\huge\bfseries hecicxna pAriBASika padagaLu}

\medskip

\begin{entry}
\word{aMgasathxla-liMgasathxla saMbaMdha}
\meaning{\arthanonum{parashivanu mAnava matutx parxpaMcavanunx saqSiTxmADida meVle adariMda dUra uLiyade, adaralelxV aMtagaRtanAgirutAtxne. manuSayxnu parashivananunx Aru sathxlagaLalilx sAkASxtAkxra mADikoLaLxbahudu. aMgana I Aru aMgasathxlagaLeMdare Bakatx, maheVsha, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa matutx aikayx. avanu sAkASxtAkxra mADikoLuLxva shivana sathxlagaLige liMgasathxlaveMba hesaridudx, avu karxmavAgi AcAra\-liMga, guruliMga, shivaliMga, jaMgamaliMga, parxsAdaliMga matutx mahAliMga enisikoLuLxtatxve. I Aru aMgasathxlagaLu\break Aru liMgasathxlagaLalilx saMbaMdha hoMdive. heVgeMdare: \hbox{manuSayxna} aMgavu parashivana shakitxya rUpAMtara. \hbox{manuSayxnu} baMdhanadalilxruvavarege aMgasathxlagaLu shakitx athavA adhoVmAye enisikoLuLxtatxve. oMdu veVLe avanu avugaLanunx AdhAyxtimxka udedxVshakAkxgi baLasidare avu Bakitx athavA UdhavxRmAye enisikoLuLxtatxve.}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad motatxmodalaneya AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka BakatxnenisikoLuLxtAtxne. parashivana kirxyAshakitxyu Bakatxnalilx GArxNeVMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx adaralilx parashivanu AcAraliMgarUpadalilx aMtagaRtavAgidAdxne. AcAra\-liMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba Bakatxnu tananx citatxvanenxV hasatx\-vanAnxgi mADikoMDu AcAraliMgakekx parimaLadarxvayxgaLanunx apiRsutAtxne hAgU A apiRtavu gaMdhaveMba parxsAdavAgutatxde. Bakatxna I Bakitxge vishAvxsaBakitx athavA sharxdAdhxBakitx athavA\break sadaBxkitx eMdu hesaru. hiVge apiRsida citatxvu sucitatxvenisi\-koLuLxtatxde. GArxNeVMdirxyadalilxruva AcAraliMgakekx avanu apiRsuvudariMda, GArxNeVMdirxyavu (mUgu) parashivana (AcAraliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.45)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
AcArAyApiRtA paqthivxV guroVrApaH samapiRtAH\\
shivAya cApiRtaM teVjashacxrAya marudapiRtaH\\
parxsAdAyApiRtaM voyxVma jiVvAtAmx mahateV\char'263piRtaH
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{BajeVta 45}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya eraDaneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhakanige maheVsha (mAheVshavxra) eMdu hesaru. parashivana jAcnxna\-shakitxyu mAheVshasathxladalilxruva sAdhakanalilx jihevxVMdirxya\-vAgi (nAlageyAgi) rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, parashivanu adaralilx guru\-liMga\-vAgi aMtagaRtavAgidAdxne. guruliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba maheVshanu tananx budidhxyanenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu, rasaveMba darxvayxvanunx apiRsi, adanunx ruciyeMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. maheVshana I Bakitxge neYSiThxkaBakitx eMdu hesaru. rasavanunx apiRsuva maheVshana budidhxge subudidhxyeMdu hesaru. nAlageyalilxruva guruliMgakekx\break avanu ruciyanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkari\-suva jihevxVMdirxyavu (nAlageyu) parashivana (guru\-liMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.46)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
AcAreV divayxliMgeV nirupamanijaBakatxsathxlAMgeYkayxBAji\\
GArxNAKeyxV citatxhasetxVna ca GanasuKaheVtw kirxyAshakitxyuketxV\\
GArxtavayxM darxvayxmapayxpaRNaviSayavidhAnoVpadiSaTxM samapayxR\\
pArxyasasxdaBxkitxpUNaR savxyamayamiha gaMdha parxsAdaM
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{BajeVta 46}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya mUraneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka\-nige parxsAdi eMdu hesaru. parashivana icACxshakitxyu \hbox{sAdhakana} neVtarxvAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige shivaliMga eMdu hesaru. shivaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisi\-koLaLxbeVkeMba parxsAdiyu tananx ahaMkAra\-vanenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu rUpadarxvayxgaLanunx shivaliMgakekx apiRsi, adanunx rUpa eMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. \hbox{parxsAdiya} I Bakitxge avadhAnaBakitx eMdu hesaru. beLakanunx apiRsuva parxsAdiya ahaMkArakekx nirahaMkAraveMdu hesaru. neVtarx\-dalilxruva shivaliMgakekx avanu rUpavanunx apiRsuvudariMda A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkarisuva neVterxVMdirxyavu (kaNuNx) parashivana (shivaliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.47)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
sAvxMgeV mAheVshavxrAtamxnayxnupamasahajajAcnxnashakitxparxyuketxV\\
jihAvxseyxV suparxsidedhxV parataraguruliMgABidheV saMsithxteV\char'263simxnf\\
niSAThxBakitxparxBAvaparxNihitasumahAbudidhxhasetxVna vidAvxnf\\
rasayxM darxvayxM samapayxR savxyamamalarasAKayxM parxsAdaM
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{BajeVta 47}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya nAlakxneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka\-nige pArxNaliMgiyeMdu hesaru. parashivana Adishakitxyu \hbox{sAdhakana} tavxgiMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathx\-vAgiruva parashivanige jaMgamaliMgaveMdu hesaru. jaMgamaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba pArxNaliMgiyu\break tananx manasasxnenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu, sapxshaRdarxvayxgaLanunx jaMgama\-liMgakekx apiRsi, adanunx sapxshaRveMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. pArxNaliMgiya I Bakitxge anuBAvaBakitx eMdu hesaru. sapxshaRvanunx apiRsuva pArxNaliMgiya manasisxge\break sumanaveMdu hesaru. tavxgiMdirxya (camaR) dalilxruva jaMgama\-liMgakekx avanu soVMkanunx apiRsuvudariMda, adanunx sivxVkari\-suva tavxgiMdirxyavu parashivana (jaMgamaliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisi\-koLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.48)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
yoV\char'263sw nitayxM parxsAdisathxlaparamapadapArxpatxdivAyxMgaBAji\\
sevxVcACxshakitxparxyuketx daqshi jagati muKeV pANinA\char'263haMkaqteVna\\
sAkASxlilxMgeV shivAKeyxV savinayamavadhAnAtamxtABakitxyukotxV\\

\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{BajeVta 48}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad aidaneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhakanige sharaNaneMdu hesaru. parashivana parAshakitxyu sharaNana shorxVterxVMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtara\-goMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige parxsAda\-liMgaveMdu hesaru. parxsAdaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisi\-koLaLx\-beVkeMba sharaNanu tananx jAcnxnavanenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu, shabadxvanunx parxsAdaliMgakekx apiRsi, sushabadxveMdu parxsAdavanunx paDeyutAtxne. sharaNana I Bakitxge AnaMdaBakitx eMdu hesaru. shabadxvanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkarisuva shorxVterxVMdirxyavu parashivana (parxsAdaliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.49)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
saMsaketxV pArxNaliMgisathxlanihitanijAMgeV manaHpANinA\char'263sw\\
liMgeV sAkASxcaCxrAKeyxV tavxci jagati muKeV hAyxdishakitxparxyuketxV\\
sapxrXSaTxvayxM cApaRyitAvx savxyamanuBavaBakitxparxBAvoVpapanonxV\\
nitayxM sapxshaRparxsAdaM niratishayasuKaM tatatxvXveVtAtx
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\pauthor{BajeVta 49}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad koneya haMtada sAdhakanige aikayxneMdu hesaru. \hbox{parashivana} citfshakitxyu aikayxna BAva(haqdaya)vAgi rUpAMtara\break\-goMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige mahA\-liMga\-veMdu hesaru. mahAliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba aikayxnu tananx BAvavanenxV (jiVvAtamxnanenxV) hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. aikayxnu toVrisuva Bakitxge samarasaBakitx eMdu\break hesaru. taqpitxyanunx apiRsuva aikayxna BAvakekx kelavu veVLe sadABxva\-veMdu kareyalAgutatxde. haqdayadalilxruva mahA\-liMgakekx avanu taqpitxyanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNe\-yanunx sivxVkarisuva haqdayavu parashivana (mahAliMgana) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde. (a.sU., 7.50)}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}

\pauthor{BajeVta 50}

%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{aMgasathxla hAgU liMgasathxlagaLa saMbaMdhavanunx yAva shakitx yAva iMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtaragoMDide muMtAda meVlina vivaragaLanunx I keLaginaMte saMkiSxpatxvAgi toVrisabahudu. (va.pA.koV.)}}
%\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\artha{piMDasathxla, piMDajAcnxnasathxla, saMsAraheVyasathxla, gurukAruNayxsathxla, liMgadhAraNasathxla, viBUtisathxla, rudArxkaSx dhAraNasathxla, paMcAkaSxriVjapasathxla, Bakitxsathxla, surUpoVBayasathxla, tirxvidhi saMpatutxsathxla, catuviRdha sArAyasathxla, upAdhimATasathxla, nirupAdhi mATasathxla matutx sahaja mATasathxla eMba 15 viBAgagaLu Bakatxsathxladalilxve.} \artha{mAheVshavxraparxshaMsAsathxla, liMganiSAThxsathxla, pUvARsharxya nirasanasathxla, vAgadevxYtanirasanasathxla, AhAvxnanirasanasathxla, aSaTxtanumUtiRnirasanasathxla, savaRgatanirasanasathxla, shivajaganamxyasathxla matutx deVhikaliMgasathxla eMba 9 viBAgagaLu mAheVshavxrasathxladalilxve.} \artha{pArxsAdisathxla, gurumAhAtamxyXsathxla, liMgamAhAtamxyXsathxla, jaMgamamAhAtamxyXsathxla, BakatxmAhAtamxyXsathxla, sharaNamAhAtamxyXsathxla matutx parxsAdamAhAtamxyXsathxla eMba 7 viBAgagaLu parxsAdisathxladalilxve.} \artha{pArxNaliMgisathxla, pArxNaliMgAcaRnasathxla, shivayoVgasamAdhisathxla, liMganijasathxla matutx aMgaliMgasathxla eMba 5 viBAgagaLu pArxNaliMgisathxladalilxve.} \artha{sharaNasathxla, tAmasanirasanasathxla, nideRVshasathxla matutx shiVlasaMpAdanasathxla eMba 4 viBAgagaLu sharaNasathxladalilxve.}
%\artha{aikayxsathxla, AcArasaMpatitxsathxla, EkaBAjanasathxla matutx sahaBoVjanasathxla eMba 4 viBAgagaLu aikayxsathxladalilxve.}}

\begin{entry}
\word{arivu kuruhu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{tiLivaLike; I iMdirxyagoVcara vishiSaTx jAcnxna; arivu uMTAguvudu ``citf"dalilx. `citf'dalilx moVha, ahaMkAra, loVBAdi guNagaLu BAvarUpadalilx nelasidare `citf' ashudadhxBAvagaLa leVpanavuMTAgi aviveVka Avarisutatxde. jiVvAtamxnu liMgavanunx kuruhu (saMkeVta) mADikoMDu sAdhanegeYdare ashudadhxBAva ilalxvAgutatxde:}
\ullekha{nenahu satitxtutx BArxMtu beMditutx arivu mareyitutx kuruhugeTiTxtutx (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 298-86); ariyade ajAcnxnadalilx kuruhu bididxtetxMdu pArxNAGAtava mADikoMDu sAva ajAcnxnigaLa noVDA! (savasaM.\break 3; cenanxba. 1275-449); neleya meVliTuTx kuruhu\-geDabalalxDe terahilalx kapilasidadhxmalilxkAjuRna (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 701-198).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{apiRtavilalxda ApAyxyini}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shivanalilx oMdAgiruva GanavAda taqpitx; liMga aMga beVreyeMdukoMDa\-vanu liMgakekx (parashivanige) halavu BakaSxyXBoVjayxgaLanunx apiRsi, avugaLanunx parxsAdaveMdu sivxVkarisi taqpitxpaDutAtxne. Adare, liMgAnuBAviyAda sharaNanu EnanUnx liMgakekx apiRsa\-deyeV, EnanUnx parxsAdaveMdu sivxVkarisadeyeV taqpitxpaTuTx\-koLuLxtAtxne:} \ullekha{kamaRvilalxda kAraNikanu, apiRtavilalxda ApAyxyani, jaMgamavilalxda samashiVlanu, liMgavilalxda nirutanu (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 759-226).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{asaMKAyxta(ru)}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shivaBakatx; sharaNaru:}
\ullekha{toreyudakava kereyuMDu taqpatxvAgalu A kereyudakava halavu kelavu sAthxvara jaMgamagaLuMDu taqpitxvaDevaMte, parxBudeVvara taqpitx asaMKAyxta mahAgaNaMgaLelalxkekx taqpitxyAyitutx noVDA (savasaM. 1; basava. 1210-333); anaMtaloVkAloVkada asaMKAyxta mahAgaNaMgaLelalxru liMgaBAvadalilx BaritarAgi, gaganasidAdhxMtadiMda upadeVshakekx baMdu BakitxrAjayxvane hokukx, nijaliMgasukeSxVtarxvane kaMDu, aKaMDa paripUNaR pUjeya mADuvavarige namoVnamoV eMbe guheVshavxrA (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 281-82); iSaTx pArxNa BAvaveMba tirxvidhaliMgasaMbaMdha beVDaveMdaDe asaMKAyxta parxmathagaNaMgaLopupxvare? kUDalacenanxsaMgayayxnalilx iSaTxliMgasaMbaMdhavilalxdavara muKava noVDalAgadu parxBuve (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1642-600); basavaNaNx, kapilasidadhxmalilxkAjuRnA, cenanxbasavaNaNxnAgi parxBu modalAgi asaMKAyxtarelalxranu toVride guruve (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 1323-382); tanu shudadhxvAyitutx shivaBakatxrokukxda koMDenanx. mana shudadhxvAyitutx asaMKAyxtara nenedenanx kaMgaLu shudadhxvAyitutx sakalagaNaMgaLa noVDi enanx (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 230-69); ele asaMKAyxtarira I huyayxlanavadharisi salahi (basapu. 44-48).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{na saMKAyxtaM - asaMKAyxtaM}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{asaMsAkxra}
\meaning{\arthanonum{viVrasheYva diVkeSxyanunx paDeyadavanu:} \ullekha{atapatxtanurajojxV veY AmaH saMsAkxravajiRtaH. viVrasheYva diVkeSxyanunx paDeyade berasidene BaviBeVda uLidanukarisi keYkoMDene asaMsAkxra racita pAkaMgaLaM parihariseneV (basapu. 44-15).}}
\newmeaning{\ni{avidayxmAnaH saMsAkxroV yasayx|}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{asithxra manasusxLaLxvanu:} \ullekha{kUDalasaMgamadeVvara Bakitx aLimanadavarige aLavaDadayAyx (savasaM. 1; basava. 668-167).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aLivu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{liMgAMgasAmarasayxvanunx sAdhisi matetx huTaTxdiruvudu:} \ullekha{aLivarige uLivu elilxyU ilalxveMdu tiLi, uLivarige aLivu elilxyU ilalxveMdu tiLi (savasaM. 8; moVLige. 1490-500).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{AkAsha}
\meaning{\arthanonum{Agasa; gagana; paMcamahABUtagaLalilx hAgU mUvatAtxru tatatxvXgaLalilx
oMdu; shabadxvu guNavU vAyxpakavU Adudu. elalx jiVvarAshigaLige avakAsha
niVDiruvudariMda AkAsha eniside. elalx iMdirxyagaLige avakAsha niVDiruvudariMda
upAdhi\-BeVdadiMda haqdayAkAsha eniside. AkAshavu budidhxtatatxvXkekx mUla AdhAra:}}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
avakAshamasheVSANAM BUtAnAM saMparxyacaCxti |\\[1pt]
AkAshaH parameVshasayx shAsanAdeVva savaRgaH ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(caM.A., kirx.pA., 1.22)}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
iMdirxyANAM tu saveRVSAmavakAshaparxdatavxtaH |\\[1pt]
haqdayAkAsha iteyxVtatf porxVcayxteV munisatatxmeYH ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 6.18)}
\smallskip
\begin{shl}
AkAsheV shabadx EveYkoV na vaNARtAmx parxtidhavxniH ||\\[1pt]
dAvxviMshateVH parasAyxsayx budidhxtatatxvXsayx kAraNamf ||
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(shi.ta.ra., BA-3, 9.3.25)}

%\begin{entry}
%\word{Adi anAdiyilalxdaMdu}
%\meaning{\arthanonum{aneVka vacanagaLu `Adi anAdi ilalxdaMdu', `Adi anAdigaLiMdatatxtatx' eMdu pArxraMBavAgutatxde. I padagaLU, saqSiTxpUvaRda parashivana sithxtige anavxyisutatxde. shivanige saqSiTxsabeVkeMba iceCxyU, tAnobabxneV idedxVneMba arivU ilalxda sithxtiyadu. idanenxV kelavu veVLe shUnayx, bayalu muMtAgi kareyalAgutatxde.}}
%\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad Adare AdiyAgali anAdiyAgali ilalxda kAla athavA vasutx EkakAlakekx iralu sAdhayxveV? parxpaMcaveV iralilalx eMdAga, AdiyuLaLx parxpaMcaviralilalx eMdathaRvAgutatxde; Adare anAdiyAda parashiva shUnayxsithxtiyalilxdadx. aMda meVle, saqSiTxpUvaR sithxtiyu Adi anAdiyilalxda kAla heVgAgutatxde eMbudeV I padaparxyoVga saqSiTxsuva samaseyx. adeV riVti, parashivaneV anAdi eMdameVle avananunx Adi anAdiyiMdatatxtatx eMdu vaNiRsuvudara athaRveVnu, eMba samaseyxyU barutatxde. I samaseyxge pArxyashaH I keLagina utatxra samapaRkavenisabahudu.}}
%\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad udAharaNege, nAvu oMdu pusatxkavanunx noVDidAga, adanunx itara pusatxkagaLoDane hoVlisi ``idU saha oMdu pusatxka'' eMdu heVLutetxVve; alalxde, paroVkaSxvAgi (hAgU mAnasikavAgi), idu kuciRyalalx, beTaTxvalalx, muMtAgiyU heVLutetxVve. parxpaMcada tuMbelalx pusatxkavalalxde matetxVnU ilalxdidadxre, adakekx `pusatxka'veMba hesaru irutitxralilalx. Adare adanunx noVDuva manuSayxneMba eraDaneV vasutxvidadxre, Aga avanu tAnu manuSayx, adu pusatxka eMdu Binanx mADutAtxne. obabx vayxkitxyanunx ``basava'' athavA ``kuLaLx'' eMdu kareyuvudu avananunx itarariMda (basavaralalxda, kuLaLxralalxdavariMda) parxteyxVkisuva saluvAgi; adeV riVti oMdu pusatxkavanunx athavA oMdu baNaNxvanunx pusatxka athavA keMpu eMdu kareyuvudu adanunx pusatxkavalalxda vasutxgaLiMda athavA keMpalalxda baNaNxgaLiMda parxteyxVkisuvudakAkxgi. hiVge hoVlike vayxtAyxsagaLanunx ariyade nAvu EnanUnx ariyalu sAdhayxvilalx.}}
%\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad adeV riVti, oMdu vasutxvanunx noVDi, idakekx Adiyide enunxtetxVve; adanunx mADidavanigU Adiyide enunxtetxVve. Adare iDiV parxpaMcavanenxV gaNanege tegedukoMDare, parxpaMcakekx Adiyide, adanunx saqSiTxsidavanige (parashivanige) Adiyilalx enunxtetxVve. Adare parxpaMcavU ilalxde, parashivanige saqSiTxsabeVkeMba iceCxyU ilalxdidAdxga, Adi-anAdi eMba joVDi padakekx A athaRkoDabahudeV? idanunx matotxMdu daqSATxMtada mUlaka pariharisabahudu.}}
%\smallskip
%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad obabx vayxkitx oMdu dhamaRkekx seVridavanAgidadxre, ``avanu viVra\-sheYvanAgirabeVku athavA viVrasheYveVtaranAgirabeVku'' enunxvudu satayx. ``avanu viVrasheYvanU alalx, viVrasheYveVtaranU alalx'' enunxvudu asatayx. oMdu veVLe A {vayxkitx} yAvudeV dhamaRkekx seVrada vayxkitx Agidadxre, ``avanu viVrasheYvanAgirabeVku athavA viVrasheYveVtaranAgirabeVku'' enunxvudu sariyalalx. adeV riVti nAvu parxpaMcavanunx noVDi, idakekx Adiyide, parashivanu anAdi enunxtetxVve. Adare parxpaMcaveV ilalxdidadxre, aMdare hoVlike vayxtAyxsagaLanunx upayoVgisikoMDu tiLiyuva manuSayxneV ilalxdidadxre, Adi anAdi eMba padagaLige athaRvilalxvAgutatxde. {aMdare} parxpaMcaveV ilalxdaMtha saMdaBaRdalilx adanunx Adi eMdu kareyabeVkAgilalx; AdiyeMdu kareyabeVkAgilalxvAdudariMda adanunx ``anAdi'' eMbudariMda parxteyxVkisabeVkAgilalx. aMdare, shUnayx kAlakekx saMbaMdhisidaMte ``Adi-anAdi'' eMba padaparxyoVga nirathaRka.}}

%\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad ``AdianAdiyilalxdaMdu'' eMbudakekx matotxMdu riVtiya athaR koDabahudu. kelavu vacanakAraru `Adi' eMbudanunx deVhaveMdU, `anAdi' eMbudanunx AtamxveMdU atheYRsutAtxre. \begin{entry}
\word{terahilalxda Gana}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{GanaveMdare citutx, arivu, parashiva. yAveraDu BwtavasutxgaLanunx tegedukoMDarU, avugaLa \hbox{madheyx} teravu irutatxde. teravilalxda yAvudeV eraDu BwtavasutxgaLanunx kalipxsikoLaLxlU sAdhayxvilalx. Adare arivu athavA citutx aKaMDavAgirutatxde. anuBAva paDedavanige elalx AtamxgaLU vishAvxtamxna BAgagaLAgi kANutatxve. aSeTxV alalx, avanige BwtavasutxgaLalilxruva citUtx kANutatxde. aMdare, elalx Atamx\-gaLu hAgU vasutxgaLalilx avanige ceYtanayxveV kANutatxde. vasutxgaLalilx aneVkate hAgU veYvidhayx kaMDarU, avugaLalilxruva citutx oMdeV; adu aKaMDa. Bwta hAgU cidavxsutx\-gaLalilx A parashivaniMdAgi Ekate mUDidAga avugaLalilx aneVkate hAgU veYvidhayx naSaTxvAguvudilalx. Adare avugaLalilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanalilx veYvidhayxte athavA aneVkate ilalx. oMdu veVLe, parashivanu kelavu vasutxgaLalilx idudx, \hbox{inunx} kelavu vasutx\-gaLalilx iradidadxre, Aga cititxgU KaMDate ide enanxbahudAgitutx.}}
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{jAcnxnigaLigU anuBAvigaLigU terahilalxda Gana kANisi\-koMDare
 ajAcnxnigaLige, vasutxgaLa aneVkate matutx veYvidhayxdiMdAgi
 terahilalxda Gana kANisuvudilalx:} \ullekha{aridu neneyalilalx, maredu pUjisalilalx, terahilalxda Ganakekx kuruhu muninxlalx (savasaM. 3; alalxma. 635-171).}}
%\newmeaning{\ni{tere (te{\re}) + hu - terahu}}
\end{entry}
%idanunx oMdu upameya mUlaka sapxSaTxpaDisabahudu. aneVka jAtiya hUgaLanunx oMdu dArada mUlaka mAle mADidAga, hUvu\-gaLu tamamx aneVkate hAgU veYvidhayxgaLanunx kaLedukoLuLxvudilalx. Adare avugaLalilxruva dAra mAtarx oMdeV. A dAradiMdAgiyeV avugaLalilx Ekate baMdiruvudu. hAgeyeV,

\begin{entry}

\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{bayalu eMba padavu yAvoMdu guNavU ilalxda parashivana saqSiTxpUvaRsithxtige anavxyavAgutatxde. avana saqSiTxnimARNa shakitxyu supatxsithxtiyalilxrutatxde. rUpu eMdare deVheVMdirxyAdigaLanunxLaLx aMga (Atamx). \meaning{\arthanonum{shivananunx kuritu mADuva varxta:} \ullekha{bAradu bAradu viSayige pashupatibarxtavu (savasaM. 1; basava. 771-196); ``barxhAmxdi pashugaLige oDeyanAda shivana saMbaMdha\-vAda SaDivxdhashiVlavanenxV aMgava mADikoMDu SaDivxdha\-varxta\-vanenxV pArxNava mADikoMDu AcarisuvaMtha AcaraNeyu" (basaTiV. {\rm\em{II,}} 153-772 TiVku).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{parxNavadaAkaqtigaLu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\artha{parxNavaveMdare, OM namaH shivAya eMba Aru akaSxrada maMtarx I maMtarxda akaSxragaLu karxmavAgi tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti-ya AkAravuLaLxvugaLAgive:} \ullekha{inunx parxNavada lakaSxNavadeMteMdaDe: parxthama tAraka savxrUpavAgihudu. divxtiVya daMDasavxrUpavAgihudu. taqtiVya kuMDalAkAravAgihudu. catuthaR adhaRcaMdarxkAkAravAgihudu. paMcama dapaRNAkAravAgihudu. SaSaThx joyxVtisavxrUpavAgihudu noVDA. idakekx IshavxroVvAca: ``parxthamaM tArakA\-rUpaM| divxtiVyaM daMDa ucayxteV| taqtiVyaM kuMDalAkAraM| catuthaR cAdhaRcaMdarxkaM|| paMcamaM dapaRNAkAraM| SaSaThx joyxVtisavxrUpakaM| iti parxNava vijecnxVyaM| yadogxVpayxM varAnaneV||" iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 501-252).} \artha{paqthivx, apupx(jala), teVjasusx, vAyu, AkAsha, AtamxgaLu karxmavAgi parxNavada tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti savxrUpagaLalilx nelesive:}
\ullekha{matatxM, A shiSayxnu ele sadugxrusAvxmi, aKaMDajoyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra utapxtayxvanu nimamx mahAvAkayxdiMda nirUpisi, nimamx sAvxnuBAvadaqkikxniMda toVralu kaMDu suKiyAdenu. inunx SaDivxdha BUtaMgaLutapxtayx nAyxsasathxlavanu nirUpiseMdu binenxYsalu, A sadugxrusAvxmi nirUpisidaradeMteMdaDe: aKaMDajoyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx AtamxnutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx AkAsha utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdArxkAdalilx vAyu utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx teVja utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada daMDakasavxrUpadalilx apupx utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada tArakasavxrUpadalilx paqthivx utapxtayxvAyitutx noVDA. idakekx citapxrXkAshAgameV: ``OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| AtAmx ceYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| AkAshaM ca samudaBxvaM|| OMkAreV cAdhaRcaMderxV ca| vAyushecxYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| teVjashecxYva samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra daMDarUpeV ca| ApashecxYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra tArakarUpeV| paqthivxshacx samudaBxvaH| iti SaSaThxBUtaM deVviV| sAthxna sAthxneV samudaBxma||" iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 502-253); A aKaMDa joyxVtimaRya\-vAgiha paramoVMkAraparxNavada tArakAsavxrUpadalilx paqthivxyeMba mahA\-BUtavihudu. A parxNavada daMDasavxrUpadalilx apupxveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx teVjaveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdarxkadalilx vAyuveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx AkAshaveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx AtamxneMba mahABUtavihudu noVDA. idakekx citipxMDAgameV: ``OMkAra tArakarUpeV| paqthivxBUtaM samAcareVtf| OMkAra daMDarUpeV ca| apupx BUta samAshirxtAH|| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| teVja\-BUtaH tathABaveVtf| OMkAra adhaRcaMderxV ca| vAyuBUtaM ca vataRteV|| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| voyxVmaBUtaM sadAshirxtAH| OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| AtamxBUtAshirxtaM tathA| iti SaSaThxBUtaM deVviV| sAthxna sAthxneV samAcareVtf||" iMteMdudAgi. aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 503-254).} \artha{Bakatx, maheVshavxra, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa, aikayx - ivarugaLu tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti savxrUpagaLiMda karxmavAgi udaBxvisidaru:} \ullekha{matatxM, A shiSayxnu ele sadugxrusAvxmi, SaDivxdhaBUtaMgaLutapxtayx nAyxsasathxlavanu nimamx mahAnuBAvavacanadiMda nirUpisi, nimamx mahAnuBAvadaqkikxniMda toVralu, kaMDu paramasuKiyAdenu. inunx BakatxmAheVshavxra parxsAdi pArxNaliMgi sharaNa aikayxrutapxtayx nAyxsa sathxlavanu nirUpiseMdu binenxYsalu, A sadugxrusAvxmi nirUpisidaradeMteMdaDe: aKaMDa joyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx aikayxnutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx sharaNanutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdarxkadalilx pArxNaliMgi utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx parxsAdi utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada daMDakasavxrUpadalilx maheVshavxra utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada tArakasavxrUpadalilx BakatxnutapxtayxvAdanu noVDA. idakekx citapxrXkAshAgamoVtatxrasAreV: ``OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| aikayxMtu samu\-daBxvaM| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| sharaNashacx samudaBxvaM|| OMkAreVcAdhaRcaMderxV ca| pArxNaliMgiV samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| parxsAdiVshacx samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra daMDakarUpeV ca| mAheVshavxra samudaBxvaH| OMkAra tArakA\-rUpeV| BakatxshecxYva samudaBxvaH| iti SaDusathxlaM deVviV| sAthxnasAthxneVSu jAyateV|| iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (\hbox{savasaM.} 13; bAlasaM. 504-254).}}
\end{entry}

\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{mAnava deVhavu paMcaBUtagaLiMda racitavAgidudx, parxtiyoMdu
 BUtakUkx obobxbabx adhideVvate athavA nAyakanirutAtxne. A nAyakaru
 deVhada vividha BAgagaLalilx nelesidAdxre:}}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad paqthivxVBUtada nAyakanAda barxhamxnu haqdayasAthxnadalilx;
 apftatatxvXda nAyakanAda viSuNxvu kaMThasAthxnadalilx; aginx\-BUtada
 nAyakanAda rudarxnu BUrxmadhayxdalilx, vAyu\-BUtada nAyakanAda
 Ishavxranu netitxyalilx matutx AkAshatatatxvXda nAyakanAda sadAshivanu
lalATadalilx idAdxre:}
\ullekha{inunx BUta\-nAyakara sAthxnaveMteMdaDe : haqdayasAthxnadalilx barxhamxnihanu, kaMThasAthxnadalilx viSuNxvihanu, BUrxmadhayxdalilx rudarxnihanu, BUrxmadhoyxVdavxRdalilx Ishavxranihanu, lalATAMtaradalilx sadAshivanihanu (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 267-116).}}
\end{entry}
